31	HELP = """
32	csv2rdf.py \
33	    -b <instance-base> \
34	    -p <property-base> \
35	    [-D <default>] \
36	    [-c <classname>] \
37	    [-i <identity column(s)>] \
38	    [-l <label columns>] \
39	    [-s <N>] [-o <output>] \
40	    [-f configfile] \
41	    [--col<N> <colspec>] \
42	    [--prop<N> <property>] \
43	    <[-d <delim>] \
44	    [-C] [files...]"
45	
46	Reads csv files from stdin or given files
47	if -d is given, use this delimiter
48	if -s is given, skips N lines at the start
49	Creates a URI from the columns given to -i, or automatically by numbering if
50	none is given
51	Outputs RDFS labels from the columns given to -l
52	if -c is given adds a type triple with the given classname
53	if -C is given, the class is defined as rdfs:Class
54	Outputs one RDF triple per column in each row.
55	Output is in n3 format.
56	Output is stdout, unless -o is specified
57	
58	Long options also supported: \
59	    --base, \
60	    --propbase, \
61	    --ident, \
62	    --class, \
63	    --label, \
64	    --out, \
65	    --defineclass
66	
67	Long options --col0, --col1, ...
68	can be used to specify conversion for columns.
69	Conversions can be:
70	    ignore, float(), int(), split(sep, [more]), uri(base, [class]), date(format)
71	
72	Long options --prop0, --prop1, ...
73	can be used to use specific properties, rather than ones auto-generated
74	from the headers
75	
76	-D sets the default conversion for columns not listed
77	
78	-f says to read config from a .ini/config file - the file must contain one
79	section called csv2rdf, with keys like the long options, i.e.:
80	
81	[csv2rdf]
82	out=output.n3
83	base=http://example.org/
84	col0=split(";")
85	col1=split(";", uri("http://example.org/things/",
86	                    "http://xmlns.com/foaf/0.1/Person"))
87	col2=float()
88	col3=int()
89	col4=date("%Y-%b-%d %H:%M:%S")
90

51	PN_LOCAL_BACKSLASH_XFAIL_REASON = """
52	    Contrary to the ratified SPARQL 1.1 grammar, the RDFlib SPARQL propcessor
53	    accepts backslashes as part of PN_LOCAL which it treats as escape
54	    characters.
55	
56	    There should be a way to instruct the SPARQL parser to operate in strict
57	    mode, and in strict mode backslashes should not be permitted in PN_LOCAL.
58	
59	    See https://github.com/RDFLib/rdflib/issues/1871
60	"""
